They are friendly and curious - typical cats! If you have problems with animals, please bear this in mind when considering my space. - Check in and check out. I'm flexible, working with my guests, on the check-in/out times. However, in the event that I have a guest leaving and another arriving on the same day, I have set the check out time at 11am.
